<script type="text/javascript">
function checkBrowserName(name)
{
    var agent = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
    if(agent.indexOf(name.toLowerCase()) > -1)
    {
        return true;
    }
    return false;
}

function isNumeric(n)
{
    return !isNaN(parseFloat(n)) && isFinite(n);
}


function getBrowserVersion(name)
{
    var agent = navigator.userAgent;
    if(name == "IE")
    {
        var ergebnis = agent.match(/MSIE [0-9\.]+/gi);
        var version = ergebnis[0].split(" ");
        return version[1];
    }
    else if(name == "safari")
    {
        var ergebnis = agent.match(/Version[/0-9\.]+/gi);
        var version = ergebnis[0].split("/");
        if(version.indexOf(".") != version.lastIndexOf("."))
        {
            version = version[1].substr(0, version[1].indexOf(".", version[1].indexOf(".") + 1));
        }
        return version;
    }
    else if(name == "chrome")
    {
        var ergebnis = agent.match(/chrome[/0-9\.]+/gi);
        var version = ergebnis[0].split("/");
        if(version.indexOf(".") != version.lastIndexOf("."))
        {
            version = version[1].substr(0, version[1].indexOf(".", version[1].indexOf(".") + 1));
        }
        return version;
    }
    else
    {
        var version = agent.match(/[0-9\.]*$/)[0];
        if(version.indexOf(".") != version.lastIndexOf("."))
        {
            version = version.substr(0, version.indexOf(".", version.indexOf(".") + 1));
        }
        return version;
    }
    return false;
}


function set_testsieger_logos()
{
    var browserversion = "undefined";
    var browserspacerbeiwert = 0;
    if(checkBrowserName("MSIE"))
    {
        browserversion = getBrowserVersion("IE");
        if(isNumeric(browserversion))
        {
            if(browserversion < 9.0)
            {
                browserspacerbeiwert = 4;
            }
        }
    }

    if(checkBrowserName("firefox"))
    {
        browserversion = getBrowserVersion("ff");
        if(isNumeric(browserversion))
        {
            if(browserversion < 10.0)
            {
                browserspacerbeiwert = 0;
            }
        }
    }

    var menue_height = document.getElementById('menue').offsetHeight;
    var content_height = document.getElementById('content').offsetHeight;
    var testsieger_content = document.getElementById('testsieger_content');
    var spacer_testsieger_content = document.getElementById('spacer_testsieger_content');
    var live_und_newsletter = document.getElementById('live_und_newsletter');
    document.getElementById('testsieger_right').innerHTML = '<img src="https://www.handyzubehoer.de/shop/images/freemenue/testsieger-hl.jpg" border="0" height="44" width="146">';
    var array_divs = new Array('<div style="float: left; width: 146px; height: 174px; text-align: left;"><img src="https:\/\/www.handyzubehoer.de\/shop\/images\/freemenue\/chip_preissieger_canon.gif" border="0" width="146" style="margin-top:5px;" alt="Logo"><br><div style="position: relative; top: 2px;"><span style="font-size:10px;font-weight:bold;line-height:10px">Patronen für Canon<\/span><br><span style="font-size:8px; font-weight: bold; line-height:10px; color: #7e7e7e;">CLI-8BK, PGI-5BK.Platz 4\/6<\/span><br><span style="font-size:10px;font-weight:bold;line-height:10px">Ersparnis: 73,68%*<\/span><br><\/div><\/div>','<div style="float: left; width: 146px; height: 174px; text-align: left;"><img src="https:\/\/www.handyzubehoer.de\/shop\/images\/freemenue\/chip_preissieger_hp.gif" border="0" width="146" style="margin-top:5px;" alt="Logo"><br><div style="position: relative; top: 2px;"><span style="font-size:10px;font-weight:bold;line-height:10px">Patronen für HP<\/span><br><span style="font-size:8px; font-weight: bold; line-height:10px; color: #7e7e7e;">Nr. 363 (-1EE, -2EE, ...).Platz 6\/7<\/span><br><span style="font-size:10px;font-weight:bold;line-height:10px">Ersparnis: 65,85%*<\/span><br><\/div><\/div>');
    var logos_ges = array_divs.length - 4;
    var computer_logo = new Array();
    for(var i = 0; i < 2; i++)
    {
        computer_logo.push(array_divs.shift());
    }
    var live_und_nl_height = live_und_newsletter.offsetHeight + 44 + 10;
    var logos_r = Math.ceil((content_height - live_und_nl_height) / 118);

    if(content_height < (logos_ges * 118))
    {
        if(logos_r < 0)
        {
            logos_r = 0;
        }
        if(live_und_newsletter.offsetHeight > 100)
        {
            var spacer_zusatz = -30;
        }
        else
        {
            var spacer_zusatz = -30;
        }
        spacer_zusatz += 20;

        logos_r += 2;
        if(logos_r > logos_ges)
        {
            logos_r = logos_ges;
        }




        var content_width = 595;

        var logo_breite = 146;

        var logos_gesetzt = 0;

        var restl_logos = logos_ges - logos_r;

        var anzahl_moegliche_logos_nebeneinander_im_content = Math.ceil(content_width / logo_breite);
        /*if(restl_logos <= anzahl_moegliche_logos_nebeneinander_im_content)
        {
            for(var j = 0; j <= logos_r; j++)
            {
                document.getElementById('testsieger_right').innerHTML = document.getElementById('testsieger_right').innerHTML + array_divs[j];
                logos_gesetzt++;
            }
            if(logos_gesetzt < logos_ges)
            {
                var spacer = (live_und_nl_height + (logos_r * 118)) - content_height + spacer_zusatz + browserspacerbeiwert + 33;
                document.getElementById('spacer_testsieger_content').style.height = Math.abs(spacer) + 'px';
                for(var j = logos_gesetzt; j < logos_ges; j++)
                {
                    var div = array_divs[j];
                    div = div.replace(/left/i, "right");
                    document.getElementById('testsieger_content').innerHTML = document.getElementById('testsieger_content').innerHTML + div;
                    logos_gesetzt++;
                }
            }
        }
        else
        {*/

            var reihen = Math.ceil(restl_logos / (anzahl_moegliche_logos_nebeneinander_im_content));

            var spacer = (live_und_nl_height + (logos_r * 111)) - content_height + spacer_zusatz + browserspacerbeiwert + 33;
            document.getElementById('spacer_testsieger_content').style.height = Math.abs(spacer) + 'px';
            var div_logos_content = '';

            for(var j = 0; j < logos_r + (reihen - 1); j++)
            {
                document.getElementById('testsieger_right').innerHTML = document.getElementById('testsieger_right').innerHTML + array_divs[j];
                logos_gesetzt++;
            }

            for(var i = 0; i <= reihen; i++)
            {
                for(var x = 1; x <= anzahl_moegliche_logos_nebeneinander_im_content; x++)
                {
                    if(logos_gesetzt < logos_ges)
                    {
                        if(x != anzahl_moegliche_logos_nebeneinander_im_content)
                        {
                            div_logos_content = div_logos_content + array_divs[logos_gesetzt];
                            logos_gesetzt++;
                        }
                        /*else
                        {
                            document.getElementById('testsieger_right').innerHTML = document.getElementById('testsieger_right').innerHTML + array_divs[logos_gesetzt];
                            logos_gesetzt++;
                        }*/

                    }

                }
            }
            for(var x = 0; x < computer_logo.length; x++)
            {
                document.getElementById('testsieger_right').innerHTML = document.getElementById('testsieger_right').innerHTML + computer_logo[x];
            }
            document.getElementById('testsieger_content').innerHTML =  div_logos_content;
        //}
    }
    else
    {

        for(var x = 0; x < array_divs.length; x++)
        {
            document.getElementById('testsieger_right').innerHTML = document.getElementById('testsieger_right').innerHTML + array_divs[x];
        }
        for(var x = 0; x < computer_logo.length; x++)
        {
            document.getElementById('testsieger_right').innerHTML = document.getElementById('testsieger_right').innerHTML + computer_logo[x];
        }
    }
}

</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
	function search_check_input ()
	{
		if (document.forms[0].elements[1].value == "Ihr Suchbegriff" || document.forms[0].elements[1].value == "" || document.forms[0].elements[1].value == " ")
		{
			alert("Bitte geben Sie einen Suchbegriff ein");
			document.forms[0].elements[1].focus();
			return false;
	    }
		return true;
	}
</script><!-- #NAG-FOOTER# -->
